<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрокинуть.html>запроки́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaprokínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрокидывать.html>запроки́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw back
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запрокинуть.html>запроки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голову</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprokínutʹ</b> golovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw back one's head</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***запрос.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запрос.html>запро́с</a> (5921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрос.html>запро́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaprós</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрос.html>запро́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрос.html>запро́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрос.html>запро́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inquiry</li>
<li>request, demand</li>
<li>query <i>(computer)</i></li>
<li><i>(plural)</i> demands, requirements, claims, interests, pretensions</li></ol>

***запросить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a> (11058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>проси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaprosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрашивать.html>запра́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inquire <i>(about, after)</i>, to request
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>све́дения</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprosítʹ</b> svédenija u kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to request information from smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprosítʹ</b> predložénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to invite offers</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to request information <i>(from)</i>, to inquire <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письменный.html>пи́сьменной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рме</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprosítʹ</b> kovó-libo v písʹmennoj fórme</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to send a written request for information</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to charge <i>(price)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слишком.html>сли́шком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорогой.html>до́рого</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprosítʹ</b> slíškom dórogo (s kovó-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask too high a price (from); overcharge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call, to request
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ввод.html>ввод</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пользователь.html>по́льзователя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprosítʹ</b> vvod dánnyx u pólʹzovatelja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prompt the user for data input</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:запросить.html>запроси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доступ.html>до́ступ</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaprosítʹ</b> dóstup (k)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seek/request access (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запротестовавший.html>запротестова́вший</a> (13445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запротестовавший.html>запротестова́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaprotestovávšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протестовать.html>протестова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">protestovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***запрягать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запрягать.html>запряга́ть</a> (22938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">запря́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaprjág-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрягать.html>запряга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaprjagátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запрячь.html>запря́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to harness (<i>a beast of burden</i>), to yoke (<i>an ox</i>)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запрятать.html>запря́танный</a> (15053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запугать.html>запуга́вший</a> (14092)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запугать.html>запуга́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapugávšij</span>)
